**能量扰动学家**：是啊，你说得没错，虚构集……\
**The Paracausality Researcher**: Yes, you're right, Recoleta.

**能量扰动学家**：我们一直都知道的，你就是这样的人，这样高尚而充满热烈情感的人。\
**The Paracausality Researcher**: There's no denying that you're a noble and passionate soul. Every one of us knows it.

**门槛旁的乞丐**：哼，我们是你最好的朋友，没有道理阻止你决定做的一切。\
**The Door-Side Beggar**: Hmph, you're our dear friend, too. Why would we stop you from doing what you truly want?

所有人都为女孩让出了道路。在她的面前，一条通往无边虚空的路出现了。\
Everyone makes way for her as a path into a boundless void unfolds.

**盲眼的织工**：我们都祝福你，由衷地为你祈祷，虚构集。\
**The Blind Weaver**: We wish you the very best, Recoleta.

**盲眼的织工**：晚安，亲爱的——祝愿这一次，你能够获得一个美好的梦境。\
**The Blind Weaver**: Goodnight, my dear. May your dream be a sweet one this time.

**虚构集**：谢谢你们，我的朋友们。我会永远想你们的。\
**Recoleta**: Thank you all, my friends. I'll never forget you.

女孩擦干眼角的泪痕，她义无反顾地迈入了黑暗之中。\
The girl wipes the tears from her eyes and steps into the looming darkness.

四周寂静得像荒芜之地的夜晚，只有轻盈的脚步声在这广袤又深邃的黑暗之中微弱回响。\
All is silent as she enters the barren land. There is only the faint sound of footsteps echoing against a vast and empty darkness.

**编辑**：虚构集小姐，我已拜读过你的作品了。坦白讲，它还没有达到足够的深度或广度。\
**Editor**: I've read your work, Ms. Recoleta. To be frank, it lacks both depth and breadth.

**编辑**：它离现实社会的复杂性还有距离，应有的锐利视角也有所缺失。希望你继续打磨，寻找让它与现实产生更强共鸣的方法。\
**Editor**: This town of yours is still far from reflecting the complexity of society, and the narrative lacks a discerning perspective. It still needs some work if you want it to truly resonate with our audience.

**编辑**：放开手做吧，年轻的作家。你正处在这样一个好年纪，一个对社会无知、好奇而四处闯荡的年纪！\
**Editor**: Just go for it, Miss. You're at a perfect age to explore, experience, and learn!

女孩第一次从虚无中感受到了自己的存在，她重拾回自己的言语。\
Time wheels, and at last the girl feels her existence again within the void. She reclaims her voice.

**虚构集**：我……发生了什么？！\
**Recoleta**: Wh-What's happening to me?

一千个，甚至无数张面孔的集合再一次浮现于眼前。\
A thousand, or perhaps countless, faces emerge before her again.

**虚构集**：哈，原来如此！《理性家族的崛起与衰落》就是“我”的故事……\
**Recoleta**: Ah, of course! The Rise and Fall of Sanity is my story.

**虚构集**：也许正是那些看过这篇小说的人，使得这个故事延续，而我也因此存在……\
**Recoleta**: So, even though the novel's been destroyed, the story—and myself along with it—lives on in the minds of those who read it.

**虚构集**：编辑先生，很感谢你的意见！即使在广袤又深邃的黑暗中，你也不忘传达你那热情的拒绝之辞！\
**Recoleta**: Thank you for your feedback, editor! Even here in this great expanse of darkness, I can still hear your words!

**虚构集**：哪怕你其实并没有理解我的小说，也永远不会看懂。但谢谢你成为了我的读者。\
**Recoleta**: You have my gratitude. Thank you for reading my novel, even if you didn't understand it and likely never will.

她在文字的迷宫与无限延展的水面中摸索着，黑暗如夜晚的海浪般向她涌来，使她的身影变得沉重。\
She navigates a labyrinth of words and an endless expanse of mirrored waters. The darkness surging toward her like a rush of waves on a dark night, making her presence feel heavier.

**同行青年Ⅰ**：说实话，我觉得听你讲故事很有意思！但我实在搞不懂这些没名字的角色之间的联系……它就不能像电影那样清晰明了吗？\
**Young Woman**: Honestly, I find your story totally fascinating! But I'm still struggling to understand the connections between all these nameless characters. Couldn't you make it clearer, like a movie?

**同行青年Ⅱ**：哼，作家都是这副德性，喜欢卖弄技巧、故弄玄虚。\
**Young Man**: Hmph, typical—trust a writer to try to be all obscure and mysterious.

**虚构集**：嘿，玛利亚，潘乔，你们是我遇到过最好的公路旅行同伴！\
**Recoleta**: María, Pancho, you guys are the best traveling pals I've ever had!

**虚构集**：即使未来的道路不同，但我们曾共同踏过草原、雪地与沙漠。我们留下了一条愉快的轨迹。\
**Recoleta**: Our paths may diverge in the future, but the joyful memories of our journey across grasslands, snowfields, and deserts together will remain forever.

**同行青年Ⅰ**：我们也很喜欢你！你是个很有趣的家伙。另外，辛勤劳动后的惬意阳光也是很棒的人生体验，我们在葡萄庄园等你过来！\
**Young Woman**: It's been great coming along with you. You're totally one of a kind. We'll be waiting for you at my aunt's vineyard. A little sun after a hard day's work will do you good.

热情的青年们朝她挥挥手，头也不回地向前走去。女孩的脚步不再虚无，每走一步，它们都变得更沉重和真实。\
The passionate companions wave to her, never looking back as they continue forward. The girl's steps are no longer weightless. With every step she takes, they feel heavier and more real.

她在无限的镜子与面具中逡巡，无限的宇宙让她陷入迷茫与虚妄。\
She lingers inside the infinite Mask in the Mirror, the boundless universe filling her with both confusion and illusion.

**理想家**：我在她的文学中感受到了尝试的姿态——它热情又破碎，混乱又诗意。但归根结底，作品整体只是一类绚烂的幻影，徒有其表，缺少了穿透灵魂的精准性。\
**The Idealist**: There is ambition in her writing. It's passionate and poetic, fractured and chaotic. But, when viewed as a whole, her work feels like little more than a superficial illusion. It lacks the depth to truly touch the soul.

**理想家**：在她停止神话自己的青春之前，我是不会给出更多评价的。\
**The Idealist**: I will refrain from offering further comments until she stops romanticizing her childish adventures.

**狱医**：坦白说，她的词句是刻意的、扭曲的。每一个词语都是一团含糊的感性泡沫。\
**The Physician**: To put it bluntly, her phraseology feels overly deliberate to the point of distortion. Her verbiage is like a collection of vague sentiment bubbles.

**虚构集**：原来如此……阿莱夫，这些都是你的真心话吗？\
**Recoleta**: I see, Aleph. Then this is how you really feel about my novel?

**阿莱夫**：在每一个读者的眼中，故事重生，人物变形，哈姆雷特不再是单一的存在，而是一千个、甚至无数张面孔的集合。\
**Aleph**: A thousand readers will interpret a story a thousand different ways. Some believe the text itself is dead, and it is the reader who gives it life.

**阿莱夫**：奥秘终归是不可被人的语言完全洞彻的。但我认为，《理性家族的崛起与衰落》是一个好故事。\
**Aleph**: The truth cannot be fully conveyed through words alone. That said, I think The Rise and Fall of Sanity is a good story.

那颗属于作家的心脏，真切地跳动起来。\
Her heart skips a beat.

在藏有无尽人类历史与奥秘的“天堂”中，她终于找到了那一面映照出真实的镜子。\
Within this "paradise" that harbors the boundless histories and mysteries of humanity, she finally finds the mirror that shows her reality as it truly is.

**虚构集**：噢，原来天堂还真长得跟图书馆差不多！还是说它只是我内心欲望的一种投影呢？\
**Recoleta**: Oh, so the eternal paradise is a library of sorts, just like I always imagined! Or, is this just another reflection of my inner thoughts?

**虚构集**：我喜欢这里，喜欢那种被文字包围的感觉。\
**Recoleta**: Hmm, I like it here. It's nice being surrounded by literature.

**虚构集**：但……我该回去了，回到现实中去。\
**Recoleta**: But it's time to go back. Back to reality.

**虚构集**：门槛旁的乞丐先生，你说得对，文学的确是无用的举动，但我相信它。\
**Recoleta**: You're right about literature, Door-Side Beggar. It is a dangerous and futile calling, but I still believe in it.

来自基金会的女孩们松了口气。\
The investigators from the Foundation breathe a sigh of relief together.

女孩的出现就像她的消失一般过于突然，第一助手还没有时间擦干净眼角的泪珠。\
Recoleta's reappearance is as sudden as her disappearance. Sonetto hasn't even had time to wipe the tears from the corners of her eyes.

**十四行诗**：虚构集……？你回来了？！\
**Sonetto**: Recoleta? You're back!

**维尔汀**：很高兴看到你平安无事。\
**Vertin**: I'm so glad to see you're safe.

**虚构集**：嘿嘿！十四行诗，维尔汀！我很高兴，原来我们有这么熟！\
**Recoleta**: And I'm so glad to see you two worried sick about me, tee-hee! Thanks, my best friends Sonetto and Vertin!

**十四行诗**：……\
**Sonetto**: ...

焕发新生的青年作家，将目光落在陷入颓丧的囚徒身上。\
The reborn writer turns to the prisoner sitting dejected nearby.

**虚构集**：看到了吗？事情并非如你所想的那样，阿莱夫。\
**Recoleta**: See, Aleph? I still exist.

**阿莱夫**：阿马尔菲塔诺消失了，一切都结束了。\
**Aleph**: Amalfitano is gone. It's all over.

**阿莱夫**：虚构集，你与那些无家可归的幽灵一样，再也无法回到故乡。\
**Aleph**: You're simply a wandering ghost now, never to return home again.

**阿莱夫**：即使你仍旧存在，你也再不能得到阿马尔菲塔诺的结局了……你否定了它，让这一切都失去了意义。\
**Aleph**: You may still exist, but Amalfitano will never get its ending. You've nullified its existence, rendering all of this meaningless.

**阿莱夫**：很抱歉，我没能解答你的问题。我又失败了……\
**Aleph**: I'm sorry I couldn't answer your question. I've failed once again.

属于魔法师的骰子跌落在地上。它曾用来搭建了一个美妙的幻梦，但如今它已经消散了。\
His die falls to the ground. Once used to construct a beautiful dream, now whatever magic it held has dissipated.

**阿莱夫**：从阿马尔菲塔诺到科马拉，一切都是一个巨大的整体。\
**Aleph**: Amalfitano and the Panopticon were two parts of a whole.

**阿莱夫**：当阿马尔菲塔诺消逝后，科马拉的一切也不需要存在……\
**Aleph**: With Amalfitano gone, Comala no longer has any reason to exist.

**虚构集**：我很遗憾，阿莱夫先生。你知晓世间所有的奥秘，寻找一切问题的回答——\
**Recoleta**: I'm sorry, Aleph. You, who know all the mysteries of the world, who seek answers to every question,

**虚构集**：但在这过程中，你唯独遗忘了你自己。\
**Recoleta**: have lost yourself in the process.

**虚构集**：你能回答所有人的问题，但唯独回答不了自己的问题。\
**Recoleta**: You can answer everyone else's questions, but never your own.

**虚构集**：那个面具下的人，究竟是谁？他还存在吗？\
**Recoleta**: Who's the person behind that mask? Is he real? Does he still exist?

**阿莱夫**：我……是谁？\
**Aleph**: Who am I?

如此沉重的故事句号，让被困于模糊幻境的囚徒感到疲惫不堪。\
The weighty ending to the story leaves the prisoner, still trapped in a blurred illusion, exhausted.

科马拉监狱发出沉重的声响，如同年迈的水车不堪重负，开始变形、消失、彻底地瓦解在精神的水流之中。\
Comala Prison groans, like an aging waterwheel struggling under its own weight, distorting, fading, and collapsing into the currents of his mind.

**维尔汀**：大家小心。这似乎是与狱医和理想家精神崩溃时一样的情况。\
**Vertin**: Stay vigilant, everyone. This is just like when the Idealist and the Physician had their meltdown.

**维尔汀**：但这次的动静，比先前要大许多……\
**Vertin**: Only this time, it seems even worse.

**虚构集**：我想……是阿莱夫主动让科马拉监狱的一切瓦解了。\
**Recoleta**: I think ... Aleph is trying to tear down the Panopticon.

倒塌的墙壁后，一个颤抖的人影隐约可见。他紧紧握着枪，漆黑的枪口随着双手晃动，朝向房间中的人群。\
Beyond the crumbling walls, a shivering figure is faintly visible. He grips a gun tightly. The black barrel, shaking in his hands, is aimed at the people in the room.

**？？？**：……等等，你们都不要动！就站在原地！\
**???**: F-Freeze! Stay where you are, all of you!

## 9TH-18 愚人颂 / In Praise of Folly

一名囚犯颤抖着从墙壁后走出，连带着手中的武器一起。\
A prisoner steps out from behind the wall, a weapon held in his shaking hand.

**加西亚**：我在展厅布展的时候，留意到监狱忽然震动了，然后我发现这并非我的幻觉。\
**García**: I was just setting up my exhibit when everything started shaking. Then I realized it wasn't just my imagination.

**加西亚**：我顺着墙壁的裂缝，找到了通往这里的路……\
**García**: So I followed the cracks in the wall and found my way here.

**加西亚**：我并非有意偷听你们的对话，但……监狱正在发生着某种变化，对吗？！\
**García**: I didn't mean to eavesdrop, but something's happening to the Panopticon, isn't it?

他神色仓惶地将枪口移向倒在一旁的阿莱夫。\
His panicked hands shift the gun toward Aleph, who has collapsed on his side.

**加西亚**：您就是狱医先生吗？……还是说，阿莱夫先生？\
**García**: Are you the Physician? Or is it Aleph?

**加西亚**：不管是谁，拜托您了，拜托了……求您让监狱恢复原样吧……\
**García**: Whoever you are, please, please restore the Panopticon to the way it was! I'm begging you!

**加西亚**：您一定……一定能做到的对吗！\
**García**: You-You can do that, right?

**阿莱夫**：……\
**Aleph**: ...

曾经创造了无限的魔法师，如今只是沉默地注视着面前所发生的一切。\
The mind that once created infinity now watches as it folds back into nothing before him.

**加西亚**：……该死，该死！怎么会这样！！\
**García**: Why? Why aren't you doing anything? Damn it! Why is this happening?

**加西亚**：对了，那个骰子在哪儿？！既然如此，我只能……\
**García**: Oh, oh, the die! If you won't help me, then I'll do it myself!

处于绝境中的囚犯冲了上来。\
The prisoner, in desperation, lunges forward.

**虚构集**：冷静点，加西亚！！\
**Recoleta**: Calm down, García!

**十四行诗**：司辰，他……\
**Sonetto**: Timekeeper, he's ...

久居监狱的囚犯被轻易地打倒在地，虚弱无力的他，甚至没能抵挡住神秘术的轻轻一击。\
García, weakened by his long confinement, is easily knocked to the ground, unable to withstand even the lightest touch of arcane skill.

**加西亚**：为什么，为什么会这样……\
**García**: Why? Why is this happening to me?

**加西亚**：我只是想完成我的展览。只差一点，另一个我只差一点的调整……\
**García**: I was so close ... so close to completing the exhibition.

**虚构集**：加西亚，你还不明白吗？控制者的消失，代表着监狱中的一切都结束了……你自由了啊！\
**Recoleta**: Can't you see, García? There is no one controlling this place now! You're free!

**虚构集**：一直以来，困住你的不是这个骰子，不是这座监狱，而是那些你没法看到的东西。\
**Recoleta**: It isn't the die that's trapped you, nor is it the walls of this prison.

**虚构集**：那些规训，那些权力的视线……它们都消失了。\
**Recoleta**: It's the rules and that overpowering gaze from the central tower, but now that's all gone.

**虚构集**：你可以去外边，去任何地方办你的展览，而不用一直被困在这个地方——\
**Recoleta**: You can go outside. You can set up your exhibit anywhere you want. No need to stay stuck in this—

失去了一切的艺术家打断了对方的话。\
Looking back on all that he has lost, the artist cuts her off.

**加西亚**：……你不懂，虚构集小姐。你从外面而来，你应该比我更清楚才对。\
**García**: No, Ms. Recoleta. You've seen the world out there. You know as well as I ...

**加西亚**：除了这里，我哪里都去不了。\
**García**: ... that there's nowhere else I can go but here.

**加西亚**：除了这里，我没有地方，可以办我的展览……\
**García**: This is the only place in the world where I can hold my exhibit.

**加西亚**：你把这一切都毁了。\
**García**: And you've ruined it. You've ruined everything.

**虚构集**：……\
**Recoleta**: ...

**维尔汀**：这个瞭望塔中的房间马上要坍塌了，我们先离开吧。\
**Vertin**: This room's about to collapse. We've got to leave.

**维尔汀**：加西亚先生，您是否需要帮助？\
**Vertin**: Mr. García, do you need a hand?

**加西亚**：……我可以自己走，谢谢你们。\
**García**: I can take care of myself, thank you.

**加西亚**：我……我要回去完成我的展览，应该与你们不同路。\
**García**: I ... I'll go a different way. I have to go back and finish setting up my exhibit.

他挪动着沉重的脚步，顺着原路离开了这里。\
He drags himself forward with trudging steps, retracing his path to leave.

**虚构集**：维尔汀，那阿莱夫呢？我们不能把他就这样丢在这儿……\
**Recoleta**: Vertin, what about Aleph? We can't just leave him here.

**维尔汀**：我们仍有一些疑问需要阿莱夫先生的解答。\
**Vertin**: Of course not. We still have questions he needs to answer.

**维尔汀**：十四行诗，我们扶起阿莱夫先生，大家一起离开这里吧。\
**Vertin**: Sonetto, help me get him up. Let's get out of here.

**十四行诗**：好的，司辰。\
**Sonetto**: Yes, Timekeeper.

颓然的囚徒略感疑惑地看向身边的第一助手。\
The dejected prisoner looks at Sonetto with confusion.

**阿莱夫**：你的言语总与所想分道扬镳。你的疑惑如此频繁，错综复杂，却也显得隐秘。\
**Aleph**: Your words are always at odds with your thoughts. You carry an ocean of questions, yet never reveal even a single drop of them.

**阿莱夫**：为何你从来不发问？对周遭发生的一切，对身边的人与事物……\
**Aleph**: Why have you never shared your doubts? Why do you stay silent in the face of everything and everyone around you?

**十四行诗**：……！\
**Sonetto**: ...!

**十四行诗**：我相信……我的使命……\
**Sonetto**: I ... I believe in my duty.

囚徒的视线转向戴帽子的女孩。\
The prisoner shifts his gaze to the other Foundation investigator.

**阿莱夫**：而能量扰动学家……我留意到，你和所有的求索者都不相同。\
**Aleph**: As for you, Paracausality Researcher. You're different from any other seeker of answers.

**阿莱夫**：即使在这样一场孤注一掷的旅途中，你也很少产生疑惑。\
**Aleph**: Even on a desperate, near hopeless journey, your heart holds little doubt.

**维尔汀**：阿莱夫先生，我想，不是每个问题都必须有答案。\
**Vertin**: Perhaps not every question needs an answer, Mr. Aleph.

**阿莱夫**：……是吗。\
**Aleph**: Is that so?

总是在解答他人问题的囚徒因此陷入了沉默之中。但遗憾的是，这次也没有人能解答他的迷思。\
The prisoner, so used to answering others' questions, seems to have run into one of his own. But unfortunately, no one is here to answer it.

## 9TH-19 科马拉诸相 / Aspects of Madness

**维尔汀**：“敬爱的兀尔德女士：”\
**Vertin**: "Dear Urd,"

**维尔汀**：“是什么让你对监狱中的一切起了兴趣？”\
**Vertin**: "Why are you so interested in the Panopticon of Comala?"

**维尔汀**：“敬爱的阿莱夫阁下：”\
**Vertin**: "Dear Mr. Aleph,"

**德洛丝**：不论是作为医生还是作家，我恐怕都难以漠视身边的种种境况，尤其在科马拉这般充满冲突与不公的场所。\
**Dores**: Whether as a doctor or a writer, I simply cannot turn a blind eye to the friction around me, especially the discord and injustice I've witnessed here in Comala.

**德洛丝**：若您能给予指点，我希望询问一个问题：有什么方法能够让这座监狱中那无休无止的纷争平息下来？\
**Dores**: So, I would ask of you a question: Is there any way to resolve the endless conflicts in this place?

**阿莱夫**：要终止这一切，必须获得一个真正的故事结局。\
**Aleph**: To put an end to this, a true ending is required.

**阿莱夫**：您的到来，使得本轮的模拟可能迎来此等结局，亦可视为一种胜利。\
**Aleph**: Your arrival has made it possible for this simulation to have an ending—or rather, a victory.

**德洛丝**：胜利是指什么呢？希望您给予更加直白的解答。如果这份胜利的代价将会侵害其他囚犯的生命，恐怕我并不能接受。\
**Dores**: What do you mean by "victory"? I'd appreciate it if you could clarify in simple terms. If this victory comes at the cost of any inmate's life, I'm afraid I cannot accept it.

**德洛丝**：另外，请您回答我另一个问题：\
若我离开，这里的故事与纷争会因此终止吗？\
**Dores**: I also have another question for you: If I leave, will the stories and conflicts here come to an end?

**阿莱夫**：重塑之手的淑女格蕾丝会为您放行。\
但这不过是历史的闭环，周而复始的故事只会在这个监狱里一直上演。\
**Aleph**: Ms. Grace of Manus Vindictae will grant you passage. But in any case, the cycle of history will continue to repeat itself in this prison, and in the entire world.

**阿莱夫**：就像我们曾经历过无数次时代的恶习那般，一切并不会停止，直至血管变成通讯电线，器官变成几何式零件，所有的一切都化作油彩。\
**Aleph**: The sins of humankind will not cease until veins turn to wires, flesh and bone to geometric shapes, and the world around us twists in the colors of an oil painting.

**德洛丝**：您的话让我感到茫然。您提到的那些事件曾出现在我的梦境中，像一段段破碎的幻想。难道它们都真实存在过吗？\
**Dores**: I must say, your words have left me rather baffled. Fragments of the events you describe often appear in my dreams. Could it be that these things really happened?

**德洛丝**：但如果它们真实地存在，为何我记不清所有的细节，只有支离的片段……？\
**Dores**: If that's the case, why can't I recall the details? Why am I left with only disconnected pieces?

**德洛丝**：无论是科马拉监狱，亦或是这些怪异的梦境，我必须让这一切停止下来……\
**Dores**: The madness in Comala, these bizarre dreams ... I must put an end to them.

**德洛丝**：我到底遗忘了什么？我的记忆被某种力量篡改了吗？我感到有某种重要的事物遗失在了时间的河流之中。也许是某个使命，也许是某种责任……\
**Dores**: What have I forgotten? Has someone or something altered my memory? I can't shake the feeling that something crucial to me has been lost in the river of time. Some kind of duty, perhaps.

**德洛丝**：如果要找回我所遗忘的一切，我应该怎么做？\
**Dores**: What should I do? How can I recapture what I've lost?

**阿莱夫**：我不会回答一个已有答案的问题。\
护送您前来的人一早就告诉了您答案，并许下了一个承诺。\
**Aleph**: I won't answer a question that already has an answer, one given to you by the person who escorted you here and made you a promise.

**阿莱夫**：您已距离那个存放真相的地点十分接近。请好好回想一下，您为何会身处此地？\
**Aleph**: You're so close to the place where the truth lies. Think carefully. Why are you here?

**维尔汀**：这些我们在瞭望塔的等候室中找到的信件，说明了一切。\
**Vertin**: These letters we found have answered a great deal, but there's still something that isn't clear.

**维尔汀**：阿莱夫先生，请你告诉我们，重塑之手究竟和德洛丝女士许诺了什么？\
**Vertin**: Mr. Aleph, what exactly did the Manus promise Dr. Dores?

**阿莱夫**：一个时代。一个能让一无所知的她，记忆起自己使命的机会。\
**Aleph**: An era. A chance for her to remember her duty.

**维尔汀**：一个时代……？\
**Vertin**: An era?

**维尔汀**：所以最后，德洛丝女士请求你将她送到哪里去了？\
**Vertin**: You helped her leave the Panopticon in the end. Where did she go?

从梦中短暂清醒过来的囚徒沉默了片刻，最后，他的视线看向了虚幻而不存在的远处。\
Momentarily roused from his dream, the prisoner looks blankly for a moment before his gaze drifts back toward the distant illusion.

**阿莱夫**：南方。\
**Aleph**: Southward.

**阿莱夫**：在那片无人的大陆上，重塑之手准备实现那个关于过去与未来的寓言。\
**Aleph**: There, on the no-man's continent, Manus Vindictae is preparing to recreate the parable of the past and future.

**阿莱夫**：一个真正属于神秘学家的时代，一段辉煌的过去，也是所有人的未来。\
**Aleph**: A glorious past and a glimmering future belonging to arcanists.

**阿莱夫**：而德洛丝女士，与这个寓言有着最深层的联系。\
**Aleph**: Dr. Dores is deeply connected to this particular parable.

**十四行诗**：重塑之手究竟在南极筹备着什么……？\
**Sonetto**: Hmm. What exactly are the Manus planning to do in Antarctica?

**十四行诗**：但德洛丝女士是主动前往南极，而并非受到了重塑之手的胁迫……\
**Sonetto**: And why would Dr. Dores go there voluntarily?

问话中得到的信息，让基金会的来客心中隐隐滋生不安。\
The information revealed stirs unease in the hearts of the investigators from the Foundation.

**维尔汀**：阿莱夫先生，请问她是什么时候启程的？\
**Vertin**: Mr. Aleph, when did Dr. Dores depart?

**阿莱夫**：那是一个同时能看到阴云与太阳的日子。\
**Aleph**: It was a day when both the clouds and sun were visible.

**维尔汀**：同时能看到阴云与太阳的日子……？所以，大概是多久之前？\
**Vertin**: A day when both the clouds and sun were visible? Could you be more specific?

**阿莱夫**：具体的……时间？\
**Aleph**: Specific? You mean the time of day?

对于能记忆世界上所有书本的每一行字的人而言，他早已丧失了对时间的感知，所能依靠的仅有文字的细节。\
His mind long ago lost any sense of time, a necessary exchange to make room for an infinite cosmos of words.

无问不答的魔法师陷入了沉默。\
He once again finds himself without an answer.

**虚构集**：同时能看到阴云与太阳……？维尔汀，我知道了！\
**Recoleta**: When both clouds and the sun were visible? Hey, Vertin, I think I know!

**虚构集**：是三天前！我在街上遇到德洛丝女士的那一天，她并不是在那时候进入监狱的。\
**Recoleta**: It was three days ago! Then, Dr. Dores wasn't going to Comala on the day I met her.

**虚构集**：那是她离开科马拉监狱，前往南极的日子！\
**Recoleta**: She was leaving. She was headed to Antarctica!

**虚构集**：同阿莱夫所说的一样，那是一个被阴云遮蔽的下午，但短暂地出了一会儿太阳……\
**Recoleta**: It was cloudy that afternoon, with a brief spell of sunshine, just like Aleph described.

**维尔汀**：德洛丝女士启程的时间离得并不远……这是一个好消息。\
**Vertin**: Then it hasn't been long since she left. Excellent news.

**十四行诗**：三天的时间……如果我们马上出发，应该仍有机会追上她。\
**Sonetto**: Three days. If we set off immediately, we might still catch up to her.

**十四行诗**：但根据我们在乌斯怀亚当地所收集的信息，重塑之手在三日前轰炸了港口的码头。\
**Sonetto**: But based on the intel we gathered in Ushuaia, Manus Vindictae bombed the entire port three days ago.

**十四行诗**：现在，没有任何一艘完整的船能够起航……也许这正是重塑之手的打算：他们想要阻止基金会的介入。\
**Sonetto**: Clearly, they wanted to prevent any interference from the Foundation. It's unlikely we'll find any functioning ships there.

**十四行诗**：我会将这里的信息回报给基金会布宜诺斯艾利斯分部。司辰，我们需要寻找别的前往方式。\
**Sonetto**: I'll report the situation to the Buenos Aires branch. Timekeeper, I'm afraid we'll have to find another way to get there.

**阿莱夫**：我有一艘船。\
**Aleph**: I have a boat.

一艘由重塑所赠送的小船。\
A small boat gifted by Manus Vindictae.

在往常的数次“暴雨”中，这位科马拉的囚徒正是搭乘它，多次应重塑的邀请前往南极大陆，以躲避回溯。\
During the past several "Storms," he has taken this boat, traveling to Antarctica at Manus Vindictae's invitation to evade the reversion.

**维尔汀**：时间紧迫，阿莱夫先生，你愿意把这艘船借给我们吗？\
**Vertin**: Could you lend it to us? The situation's urgent, Mr. Aleph.

古老高耸的灯塔旁，一艘破旧不堪的小船正在海浪中摇晃。\
Beneath a decrypted lighthouse, a battered little boat bobs in sync with the waves.

它看起来如此的渺小，如此的脆弱，仿佛下一个瞬间就会被无情的冰流吞没。\
It is small and fragile, not the kind that seems capable of braving an icy sea.

**阿莱夫**：这艘船会自动将你们送至麦克默多港口，重塑之手在南极罗斯海建立的登陆点。\
**Aleph**: This boat will automatically take you to McMurdo Port, the landing point Manus Vindictae established by the shores of the Ross Sea.

第一助手将信将疑地打量着面前的小船。她对这位重塑之手的“顾问”并无太多的信任。\
Sonetto eyes the boat with skepticism, rightfully distrusting this "advisor" of Manus Vindictae.

**十四行诗**：这艘小船，是重塑的工艺吗？它的神秘学能源十分不稳定……\
**Sonetto**: This looks like Manus technology. Its arcane energy source is highly unstable.

**十四行诗**：司辰，也许我们在乌斯怀亚等待基金会的救援会比较好。\
**Sonetto**: Timekeeper, I suggest we wait for support in Ushuaia.

**虚构集**：我很少有认同十四行诗的时候，但不得不说，对于这艘小船能否安全跨越南极周围的洋流，我也持怀疑态度。\
**Recoleta**: I don't usually agree with Sonetto, but I have to admit, I don't have much confidence that a boat this small can actually make it to Antarctica.

**维尔汀**：阿莱夫先生，你知道重塑之手筹备的仪式，现在进行到何种地步了吗？\
**Vertin**: Mr. Aleph, do you know anything about Manus Vindictae's ritual? How far has it progressed?

**阿莱夫**：仪式随时会开始——我想，这是重塑之手撤离科马拉监狱的理由。\
**Aleph**: The ritual could begin at any moment. I believe that's why they left Comala.

**阿莱夫**：在重塑之手离去之时，名为淑女格蕾丝的信徒告诉我，他们会封锁这片海面。\
**Aleph**: Upon departure, one of their members, a woman named Grace, told me they would seal off the sea.

**十四行诗**：怎会如此，已经来不及了吗……\
**Sonetto**: Are we too late?

**阿莱夫**：如果你们想要找到德洛丝女士，你们就必须踏上这条相同的道路。\
**Aleph**: If you wish to find Dores, you must follow the same path she took.

沉默的时刻，只有汹涌的海浪一如既往，如同某种循环往复的预示。\
The distant drone of the raging waves fills their background like a repeating omen.

**维尔汀**：我明白了。阿莱夫先生，后续会有基金会分部的成员前来，对你的行为与病情进行评估，希望你也能耐心地回答他们的问题。\
**Vertin**: I see. Mr. Aleph, members of the Foundation branch will arrive soon to evaluate your condition. I hope you'll answer their questions with the same patience you showed us. Thank you.

**维尔汀**：十四行诗，我们出发吧。\
**Vertin**: Sonetto, let's go.

**十四行诗**：……好的，司辰。\
**Sonetto**: Yes, Timekeeper.

同往常一样，第一助手依旧没有提出自己的疑问。\
As always, Sonetto keeps any mission-irrelevant queries to herself.

准备启航的女孩们转向一旁的青年作家。\
The girls preparing to set sail turn to the young writer beside them.

**维尔汀**：也感谢你这段时间的协助，虚构集。也许你对加入基金会——\
**Vertin**: Thank you for your assistance too, Recoleta. Perhaps you'll consider joining the—

就在此时，身后传来了建筑物轰然崩塌的巨大声响。\
A thunderous crash echoes from behind them—the sound of a collapsing building.

**虚构集**：发生了什么？！这个方向是……科马拉监狱！\
**Recoleta**: What was that? It came from the Panopticon!

## 9TH-20 灰烬安放地 / In the Place of My Ashes

熊熊烈火映照在每一个人的眼瞳里——就如同这座岛屿名字的由来一样。\
Blazing flames reflect in their eyes, just like the name of this island might suggest.

冬夜燃起的火光之中，科马拉监狱的每一块砖石都在脱落、崩塌，朝着无可挽回的方向溃败。\
A winter night stands sentinel over a great conflagration as every brick of Comala Prison crumbles and falls.

**虚构集**：离开了阿莱夫的控制，科马拉监狱正在瓦解……\
**Recoleta**: With Aleph's control gone, Comala is collapsing.

**虚构集**：那些囚犯，他们并不是真正的犯人对吗……他们还不知道发生了什么事情！他们不知道监视视线的消失，也不知道操纵者的离开。\
**Recoleta**: The inmates aren't even real criminals, are they? And they're still in there, with no clue that they're no longer being watched from the central tower!

**虚构集**：需要有人告诉他们这个消息，得让他们到安全的地方去……\
**Recoleta**: We have to go tell them! We have to get them to safety!

**维尔汀**：我们要设法保障监狱中人员的安全。至少，得等到官方救援人员的到来。\
**Vertin**: Yes, we should help them get out, at least until support arrives.

**维尔汀**：但重塑之手的仪式……\
**Vertin**: But the Manus ritual ...

那艘破败的小船在众人的视线中摇晃着。\
The battered boat sways within their sight.

**虚构集**：我会回科马拉监狱去的。\
**Recoleta**: Don't worry. I'll go alone.

**维尔汀**：嗯……？\
**Vertin**: Huh?

**虚构集**：维尔汀，你们抓紧时间出发吧！当这儿的一切都结束之后，我会给你写信的，我亲爱的朋友！\
**Recoleta**: You should hurry. When this is all over, I'll write to you, my dear friend!

**虚构集**：这一路上我们都配合得如此天衣无缝，你该把这个任务放心地交给我！\
**Recoleta**: During this journey together, our teamwork has been impeccable. So, you can trust me to do this.

**虚构集**：这不仅仅是协助你们，也和你们背后所代表的组织无关。因为监狱中的囚犯们，也都是我的朋友……\
**Recoleta**: I'm not doing it just to help you or the organization you represent. I'm doing it because the inmates are my friends.

**维尔汀**：我相信你。\
**Vertin**: Okay. I trust you.

**维尔汀**：在救援中，请注意自己的安全，虚构集。\
**Vertin**: Take care of yourself, Recoleta.

**十四行诗**：如果真如狱医所说，“暴雨”即将来临，虚构集小姐，你……\
**Sonetto**: But if the "Storm" truly is imminent, as Dr. Merlin said, then, Ms. Recoleta, you'll ...

比谁都更清楚基金会那些繁复条例的第一助手陷入了沉默。她知晓，身处时代之中，面对那些对真相一无所知的神秘学家，她一个字都不能多说。\
Sonetto, more familiar than anyone with the Foundation's exhaustive regulations, has no ready answer. She knows that, in this era, before those arcanists who remain ignorant of the truth, she must watch her words.

**虚构集**：虽然我不知道你们提到的“暴雨”究竟是什么，但别担心！对一位作家来说，所有新奇的冒险都再好不过了！\
**Recoleta**: I don't quite understand what this "Storm" is all about, but don't worry. A brand-new adventure is the best thing that can happen to a writer.

**虚构集**：嗯，我想，没有什么比这两天的经历更具有传奇色彩了，我要把这一切都写进我的新小说里，包括你们大家……\
**Recoleta**: And I doubt it'll surpass the epic adventures we've shared over the past couple of days. I'm going to write everything, including the two of you, into my new novel.

**维尔汀**：你的新小说，我们是否能成为它的第一批读者？\
**Vertin**: Then I'd like to be the first to read this new novel, if that's alright?

**虚构集**：当然！我相信文字是一条跨越时间与空间的河流。\
**Recoleta**: Of course. Listen, I believe literature is like an endless, timeless river.

**虚构集**：维尔汀，总有一天，我们会在别人的故事里再次相遇的。\
**Recoleta**: So we'll meet again someday, somewhere, probably in someone else's story. Who knows?

她最后看了一眼这些可爱的新朋友们，就像她们已经认识了数十年一样。\
She takes one last look at her new friends, feeling a longing as if they had known each other for decades.

女孩头也不回地跑向燃烧中的科马拉监狱。\
Then, without a backward glance, the girl sprints back to the burning ruins of the prison.

**虚构集**：再见了，我的朋友！\
**Recoleta**: Farewell, my cherished friends!

远方的风中传来你的呼唤Escucho algo en la distancia\
I hear a sound in the distance

在黑暗中照亮我梦想的前路que me indica el camino a la fantasia\
Guiding me on to a land of existence

我将前往没有悲伤的旅途y emprendo mi andar a una ruta real\
So I journey on to a path that feels real

你的呼唤让我前行hay una voz llamandome\
There is a voice that's calling me

归于永恒的国度a otro lugar\
To somewhere far—

怜爱吧ten piedad!\
Have mercy, please!

我衷心赞颂 你的幸福Por la felicidad yo te canto\
For happiness, I sing to you

我衷心赞颂 你的自由y por la libertad yo te canto\
And for freedom, I sing to you

无人能阻止我燃烧的心灵nada podrá parar ni vencer mi ser\
Nothing can break me, nothing bring me down

如故事的回忆中 我轻盈地奔跑 跳跃着como en la infancia voy saltando\
Like a child I leap around

我衷心赞颂 你的幸福Por la felicidad yo te canto……\
For happiness, I sing to you ...

所有的访客都相继离去了。\
All the visitors depart one after another.

在遥遥传来的歌声里，监狱的“造物主”静静地望着起火的建筑。\
Amid the distant echo of singing, the "creator" of this prison stares into the fire as it burns.

直至气喘吁吁的美洲豹出现在码头的一侧。她惊疑不定地看着面前的人类。\
The moment holds for a time, until a breathless jaguar appears at the dock's edge, staring at the human before her with uncertainty.

**狱卒**：梅林先生……您是梅林先生对吗？！终于找到您了！\
**Jailer**: Dr. Merlin. You're Dr. Merlin, right? I finally found you.

**狱卒**：瞭望塔里究竟发生了什么事情……？在我离开房间不久后，监狱忽然就开始崩塌，瞭望塔也不复存在了……\
**Jailer**: What on earth happened in the central tower? Right after I left, the whole Panopticon started collapsing. The tower's in ruin.

**狱卒**：我找了很久，终于在这里找到了您。请随我来，梅林先生，这里并不安全——\
**Jailer**: I've been looking for you everywhere. Please, sir, come with me. It isn't saf—

**阿莱夫**：没必要了。\
**Aleph**: That won't be necessary.

**阿莱夫**：雪还没有停，迷宫的一切却早已付之一炬。\
**Aleph**: The snow is still falling, yet everything in the labyrinth has already gone up in flames.

**阿莱夫**：所有吉凶祸福，命运的奥秘，都只是一场荒谬的玩笑。\
**Aleph**: Fortune, fate, karma—They're nothing but a ridiculous joke.

**阿莱夫**：丢失了自己记忆、身份和名字的美洲豹，一切都结束了。你不再是被困在科马拉的狱卒。\
**Aleph**: It's over, jaguar. You have lost your memories, your identity, your name, and now, your title. You are no longer a jailer trapped in the Panopticon.

**狱卒**：……梅林先生，我听不懂您在说什么。\
**Jailer**: I don't get it, Dr. Merlin. What are you talking about?

狱卒后退了一步。属于大型捕食者的直觉让她本能地抗拒接下来的话。\
The jailer takes a step back, her predator instincts sensing the danger in the words to come.

她有预感，那会击碎她一直以来的信仰，还有她习以为常的生活。\
The damage may not be physical, but it threatens to shatter what little faith she has left to hold onto, and the life she has always known.

**狱卒**：我、我要回去科马拉监狱了。我需要回去维持监狱的秩序，防止囚犯们趁乱逃跑……\
**Jailer**: I'm-I'm going back to Comala. Order must be maintained. The prisoners mustn't be allowed to escape.

**狱卒**：我先走了，梅林先生，您多保重……\
**Jailer**: Please take care, Dr. Merlin.

仓惶犹疑的狱卒忍受着烈火的高温，往监狱的方向奔去。\
Nerves torn between panic and hesitation, the jailer at last turns toward the searing flames.

**狱卒**：嘿，你！不要乱跑，这很危险！！\
**Jailer**: Hey, you! Don't run off like that. It's dangerous!

无人顾忌她的呐喊。\
No one heeds her cries.

一个又一个的囚犯夺路而逃，面色惊慌地逃离这座崩塌中的古老迷宫。\
One prisoner after another flees in terror, escaping the crumbling labyrinth.

**囚犯Ⅰ**：我们在荒漠，在恒星，在迷宫……！\
**Inmate I**: In deserts, in stars, in labyrinths!

**囚犯Ⅱ**：我们在村庄，做梦，与死亡贴脸颊……！\
**Inmate II**: We dream on death's straw pillow!

狱卒如同一条在海浪中彷徨的小舟，完全无法把握行进的方向。终于，一个瘦弱无力的囚犯被美洲豹扑倒在地。\
The jailer drifts through the raging scene, unable to steer a sensible course. At last, she pins down a frail and powerless prisoner beneath her weight.

**狱卒**：快停下！！\
**Jailer**: Stop!

**？？？**：放过我！我想要离开……\
**???**: Get off me! Let me go!

**？？？**：你没看到吗，这里太危险了！监狱已经快崩塌了！！\
**???**: Are you blind? The Panopticon is falling apart!

**狱卒**：……是你，罗贝托。\
**Jailer**: It's you, Roberta.

狱卒认出了这名被制住的囚犯。\
The jailer recognizes the prisoner under her grip.

罗贝托，美洲诗社的成员，一个在监狱中热心、善良、安分守己的囚犯。一个逃跑的囚犯。\
Roberta, a kind and quiet prisoner, always well-behaved, now panicked and desperate to escape.

**罗贝托**：他们……他们都疯了！我早就知道，他们本来就是疯子……！\
**Roberta**: They're all mad! I knew it. They've been insane from the start!

**罗贝托**：这里已经着火了，他们还不愿意离开，还念叨着那些无人在意的东西……\
**Roberta**: The whole place is burning to the ground, and they still won't leave! They're still talking and talking about things that no one cares about.

**罗贝托**：我……我帮不了他们，我也没法帮他们，我从来都不理解那些他们提到的玩意儿，什么韵律、派系、主义……\
**Roberta**: Ah! I can't help them. I've never understood what they were talking about—the rhythms, the factions, the ideologies ...

**罗贝托**：是的，诗社的一切都很好，理想家先生人也很好，但我受够监狱了，我受够科马拉的一切了……\
**Roberta**: Yes, the people were nice, the Idealist, too, but I've had enough of this prison. I've had enough of the Panopticon.

她趴在地上痛哭着。\
She collapses onto the ground, sobbing.

**罗贝托**：我后悔了，从一开始，我就不该参加那些运动的，那些反抗根本毫无意义！！\
**Roberta**: I never should've joined these movements. It was all meaningless from the beginning.

**罗贝托**：我想去欧洲，去西班牙或者法国，我不要待在这儿了……我想回到玛格达莱娜身边。\
**Roberta**: I wanna leave this place—go to Spain or France, anywhere but here. I want to go back to Magdalena.

**狱卒**：啊……\
**Jailer**: Huh ...

美洲豹移开了制住囚犯的爪子。对方头也不回地离开了这里。\
The jaguar releases her grip. Without a backward glance, Roberta leaves.

狱卒走进了这栋她最熟悉的环形建筑。\
The jailer steps back into the circular structure she knows as her only home.

我衷心赞颂 你的幸福\
For happiness, I sing to you

我衷心赞颂 你的自由\
And for freedom, I sing to you

无人能阻止我燃烧的心灵\
Nothing can break me, nothing bring me down

夜幕下，她看到科马拉监狱如同一堆明亮的篝火，闪烁着前所未有的、撼动人心的亮光。\
Under the night sky, she sees Comala Prison glowing like a brilliant bonfire.

**狱卒**：♫……\
**Jailer**: ♫...

三天前\
Three days ago

**德洛丝**：那么，它给你带来了一种怎样的感受呢？\
**Dores**: But how does literature make you feel?

**虚构集**：……感受吗？有时我觉得自己像个学习口语的孩子，正努力地念出书本第一页的第一个词汇。\
**Recoleta**: As though I'm a kid looking through a kaleidoscope for the first time.

**虚构集**：等等，这个比喻也许并不恰当，需要更为精妙、更为直观的……\
**Recoleta**: Well, maybe that's not the best way to put it. Perhaps something a little more subtle.

在青年作家陷入文字的漩涡之时，盲眼的女士已经独自走远了。\
The young writer drowns in the vortex of words as the blind woman walks away.

她静静地朝着科马拉监狱的方向走去，来到了藏匿在悬崖与礁石后的码头。\
She walks silently toward Comala Prison, arriving at the dock hidden between cliffs and reefs.

在那儿，解答疑惑的囚徒正等待着她的到来。\
There, the prisoner who answers all questions awaits her arrival.

**德洛丝**：一艘船。去往一片陌生的土地。\
**Dores**: A ship sailing to an unfamiliar land.

**德洛丝**：……一个代表过去与未来的寓言，一个曾经存在、即将到来的时代。\
**Dores**: A parable of the past and future. An era that once existed and is yet to come.

**德洛丝**：这就是您所提供的回答吗，阿莱夫先生？\
**Dores**: Is this the answer you've provided, Mr. Aleph?

**阿莱夫**：不，兀尔德女士，这是一个需要您自己去寻找的回答。\
**Aleph**: No, Urd. You will have to find this answer yourself.

**阿莱夫**：没有人能帮助您。没有人。\
**Aleph**: No one can help you with this—no one.

**德洛丝**：我明白了。谢谢您，阿莱夫先生，我会记住您所对我说的话。\
**Dores**: I see. Thank you, Mr. Aleph. I will remember what you've told me.

因此柏拉图年<So the platonic year>\
So the platonic year

席卷出新的是非观<Whirls out new right and wrong,>\
Whirls out new right and wrong,

而卷入旧的观念<Whirls in the old instead;>\
Whirls in the old instead;

所有人都是舞者，他们的舞步<All men are dancers and their tread>\
All men are dancers and their tread

迈入了野蛮铿锵的锣鼓声<Goes to the barbarous clangour of a gong.>\
Goes to the barbarous clangour of a gong.

威廉·巴特勒·叶芝：《一九一九年》\
W.B. Yeats—Nineteen Hundred and Nineteen
